tbm_grant_air_cas_great_war = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_great_war value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
            check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1922 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            has_country_flag = tbm_cat_cas
            check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            check_variable = { var = tbm_air_competence value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_great_war value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1922 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            tbm_grant_air_cas_y1922_great_war = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_great_war value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1936 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            tbm_grant_air_cas_y1936_great_war = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_great_war value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1940 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            tbm_grant_air_cas_y1940_great_war = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_great_war value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1944 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            tbm_grant_air_cas_y1944_great_war = yes
        }
    }
}

tbm_grant_air_cas_y1922_great_war = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_great_war value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
            check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1922 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            has_country_flag = tbm_cat_cas
            check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            check_variable = { var = tbm_air_competence value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { has_tech = early_bombs }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_great_war value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1922 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_air_competence value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                has_country_flag = tbm_cat_cas
                has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
            }
            set_technology = { early_bombs = 1 popup = no }
            add_to_variable = { tbm_grant_counter_great_war = 1 }
            tbm_handle_tech_grant_notification = yes
        }
    }
}

                NOT = { has_tech = flexible_line }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_great_war value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_industry value = 1943 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_industry_competence value = 15 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                has_country_flag = tbm_cat_industry
            }
            set_technology = { streamlined_line = 1 popup = no }
            add_to_variable = { tbm_grant_counter_great_war = 1 }
            tbm_handle_tech_grant_notification = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { has_tech = concentrated_industry5 }
                NOT = { has_tech = dispersed_industry5 }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_great_war value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_industry value = 1943 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_industry_competence value = 15 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                has_country_flag = tbm_cat_industry
            }
            set_technology = { concentrated_industry5 = 1 popup = no }
            add_to_variable = { tbm_grant_counter_great_war = 1 }
            tbm_handle_tech_grant_notification = yes
        }
        else_if = {

                NOT = { has_tech = dispersed_industry5 }
                NOT = { has_tech = concentrated_industry5 }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_great_war value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }

                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_industry value = 1943 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_industry_competence value = 15 compare = greater_than_or_equals }

                check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_naval_competence value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                has_country_flag = tbm_cat_submarines
                has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
            }
            set_technology = { basic_submarine_snorkel = 1 popup = no }
            add_to_variable = { tbm_grant_counter_great_war = 1 }
            tbm_handle_tech_grant_notification = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { has_tech = improved_submarine_mtg }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_great_war value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_naval value = 1940 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_naval_competence value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                has_country_flag = tbm_cat_submarines
                has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
            }
            set_technology = { improved_submarine_mtg = 1 popup = no }
            add_to_variable = { tbm_grant_counter_great_war = 1 }
            tbm_handle_tech_grant_notification = yes
        }
        if = {

                NOT = { has_tech = improved_submarine }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_great_war value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_naval value = 1940 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
